    ADD CONSTRAINT board_like_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( member_mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

ALTER TABLE board
    ADD CONSTRAINT board_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( member_mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

ALTER TABLE class
    ADD CONSTRAINT class_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( member_mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

ALTER TABLE comments
    ADD CONSTRAINT comment_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( member_mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

ALTER TABLE license
    ADD CONSTRAINT license_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

ALTER TABLE reservation
    ADD CONSTRAINT reservation_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;

    ADD CONSTRAINT result_member_fk FOREIGN KEY ( mem_id )
        REFERENCES member ( mem_id )
    NOT DEFERRABLE;
